O you who believe! When you speak with the Messenger in private, spend something in charity before the consultation. That will be best for you, and most helpful towards purity (of conduct). But if you do not find, (the means to spend in charity), then verily, Allah is Often Forgiving (Ghafoor), Most Merciful (Raheem)
Is it that you are afraid of spending sums in charity before your private consultation (with the Prophet)? If (that is the case), then, you do not do so, and Allah forgives you, but, establish regular prayer; Practice regular charity; And obey Allah and His Messenger. And Allah is Well-Acquainted (Khabir) with all that you do
Do you not turn your attention to those who seek (friendship) of such (people) that have the anger of Allah upon them? They are neither of you nor of them, and they swear to falsehood knowingly
Allah has prepared for them a severe Penalty: Evil indeed are their deeds
They have made their oaths a screen (to hide their misdeeds): Thus they obstruct (men) from the Path of Allah. Therefore they shall have a shameful penalty
Their wealth and their sons will not be of any profit to them, against Allah; They will be companions of the Fire, to live in there (for ever)
On the Day, when Allah will raise all of them up (for Judgment): Then they will swear to Him as they swear to you: And they think that they have something (to stand upon). No indeed! They are liars
The Satan has taken the better of them. So he has made them forget the remembrance of Allah. They are the party of the Satan. Truly, it is the party of the Satan that will perish
Verily, those who oppose Allah and His Messenger they will be among those most humiliated
Allah has affirmed (and decreed): "Verily, it is I and My messengers who must win (prevail):" Verily, Allah is One full of Strength, Almighty (Able to make His Will become reality)
You will not find any people who believe in Allah and the Last Day, loving those who oppose Allah and His Messenger, even though they were their fathers, or their sons, or their brothers, or their kindred (by blood relationship). For such (people who believe) He (Allah) has written Faith in their hearts, and (He has) strengthened them with a spirit from Himself. And He will admit them to Gardens beneath which rivers flow, to live in there (for ever). Allah will be well pleased with them, and they (will be well pleased) with Him. They are the party of Allah. Truly, it is the party of Allah who will be successful (and the ultimate happiness)
Whatever is in heavens and whatever is on earth, glorifies and Praises Allah: And He is the Exalted in Might (Al-Aziz, and) the All Wise (Al-Hakeem)
It is He, Who got out the unbelievers among the People of the Book (Scripture) from their homes at the first gathering (of the forces). You did not think that they would get out: And they thought that their fortresses would defend them from Allah! But the (anger of) Allah came to them from sources that they had not expected, and He cast fear into their hearts, so that they demolished their houses by their own hands, and by the hands of the believers. Take warning, then, O you (people) with eyes (to see)
And, if Allah had not decided exile (and banishment) for them, He would certainly have punished them in this world: And in the Hereafter they shall have the punishment of the Fire
That is because they opposed Allah and His Messenger: And if anyone opposes Allah, then surely, Allah is severe in punishment
Whether you (O Muslims!), cut down the tender palm—trees, or you left them standing on the roots, it was the willingness of Allah, and (it was) because He might cover with shame those who exceed their limits
And what (booty) Allah has (taken) from them and granted to His Messenger,— Towards this (cause) you provided neither horses nor camels: But Allah gives power to His messengers over anybody He pleases; Verily, Allah is Able (Khadir) to do all things
What Allah has granted (as booty) to His Messenger (and taken away) from the people of the townships, —Belongs to Allah, to His Messenger, —And to relatives and the orphans, the needy and the wayfarer; In order that it may not (merely) be circulated between the wealthy among you. So take what the Messenger gives to you, and deny yourselves that which he withholds from you. And fear Allah; For Allah is Strict in punishment
(Some part of the booty is due) to the needy emigrants (those who came from Makkah), those who were expelled from their homes and their property, while seeking Grace from Allah, and (His) Good Pleasure, and helping Allah and His Messenger (the Prophet): Such are indeed the sincere ones:—
And (it is also for) those who before them, had homes (in Medinah) and had adopted faith (in Islam)— Show their affection to those who came to them for refuge, and entertain no desire for things in their hearts, (and had) given to the (refugees), and give them preference over themselves, even though poverty was their (own lot), and those saved from the selfishness of their own souls— Such are they, the ones who are successful
And those who came after them say: "Our Lord! Forgive us, and our brethren who came before us into the Faith (of Islam), and leave not in our hearts, hate (or sense of injury) against those who believed. Our Lord! You are indeed Full of Kindness (Ra'uf), Most Merciful (Raheem)
Have you not seen the hypocrites say to the disbelieving brethren among the People of the Book (Scripture)? "If you are forced out, we will also go out with you, and we will never listen to anyone about your affair; And if you are attacked (in fight) we will help you." But Allah sees that they are indeed liars
Surely, if they are forced out, never will they go out with them; And if they are attacked (in fight) they will never help them; And if they do help them, they will turn their backs; And they will not be victorious
(Verily), you are stronger in their breasts (and hearts of hypocrites) than Allah (because of victories won by you). That is because they are men without understanding (for the Supreme Power of Allah)
They will not fight you (even) together, except in fortified townships, or from behind walls. Their fighting (spirit) is strong among themselves: You would think they are united, but their hearts are divided. That is because they are a people who understand not
They are like those who recently came before them, they have tasted the evil result of what they did; And (in the Hereafter there is) a painful penalty for them
(Their friends deceive them), like the Satan, when he says to man, "Deny Allah," but when (man) denies Allah, (the Satan secretively) says, "I am free of you, I do fear Allah, the Lord of the Worlds (Rub-ul-'Ala'meen)
So the end of both will be that (both) go into the Fire, to live in there, for ever. Such is the reward for the wrongdoers
O you who believe! Fear Allah, and let every soul look to what it has put forward for the future. Yes, fear Allah! Verily, Allah knows well (all) that you do
And you do not be like those who forget Allah; And He caused them forget their own souls! Such are those who are rebellious
The companions of the Fire are not equal to the companions of the Garden; They will achieve the true happiness
If We sent down this Quran on a mountain, surely, you would have seen it humble itself and split open with the fear of Allah. Such are the examples that We offer men that they may (deeply) think
Allah is He, other than Whom there is no other god:— The All Knowing (Aa'lam), of the hidden and open, He, (is) the Most Gracious (Ar-Rahman), the Most Merciful (Ar-Raheem)
Allah is He, Other than Whom there is no other god:— The Sovereign Ruler (Al-Malik), the Holy One (Al-Qudus), the Source of Perfection (and Peace, As-Salaam), the Guardian of Faith (Al-Mu'min), the Preserver of Safety (Al-Muhaymin), the Exalted in Might (Al-Aziz), the Compeller (Al-Jabbar), the Supreme and Majestic (Al-Mutakabbir). Glory to Allah! (High is He) above the partners they give to Him
He is Allah, the Creator (Al-Khaliq), the Evolver (Al-Bari), the Grantor of Forms (Al-Musawwir) to Him belong the Most Beautiful Names. Whatever is in the heavens and on earth, declares His Praises and Glory, and He is the Exalted in Might (Al-Aziz), the All Wise (Al-Hakeem)
O you who believe! Do not take My enemies, and yours, as protecting friends (or protectors by) offering them (your) love, even though they disbelieve the Truth that has come to you: And have (on the contrary) driven the Messenger (the Prophet) and yourselves (from your homes), (simply) because you believe in Allah, your Lord. If you have come out to strive in My Way (Cause) and to seek My Good Pleasure, (take them not as protectors); Holding secret conversation of love with them: For I (Allah) completely know what you hide, and all that you reveal. And any of you who does this has strayed from the Straight Way
Should they gain an upper hand over you, they would treat you as enemies, and stretch forth their hands and their tongues against you with evil, and they desire that you should be disbelievers (and reject the Truth)
Neither your relative, nor your children will benefit you on the Day of Judgment; He will judge between you: And Allah is All Seeing (Baseer) of all that you do
Indeed for you, there is, an excellent example in Ibrahim (Abraham) and those with him, when they said to their people: "Verily, we have rejected you, and whatever you worship besides Allah. We have disbelieved you, and there has arisen, between us and you, a hostility and hatred for ever— Unless you believe in Allah and Him Alone." But (it was) not so when Ibrahim (Abraham) said to his father: "Verily, I will pray for forgiveness for you, though I have no power (to get) anything on your behalf from Allah." (They prayed) "Our Lord! In You do we trust, and to You do we turn in repentance, and to You is (our) final return
Our Lord! Do not make us a (test and) trial for the unbelievers, but forgive us, our Lord! Verily, You are the Exalted in Might (Al-Aziz), the Wise (Al-Hakeem)
Certainly, there is indeed, in them an excellent example for you to follow— (And) for those who await the meeting with Allah and believe in the Last Day. And if any turn away, then truly, Allah is free of all wants, worthy of all Praise
It may be that Allah will grant love and friendship between you and those whom you (now) hold as enemies, and Allah has the Power (over all things): And Allah is Often Forgiving (Ghafoor), Most Merciful (Raheem)
Allah does not forbid you to act justly and kindly with those (for friendship) who do not fight with you regarding (your) faith (of Islam), and do not drive you out of your homes. Verily, Allah loves those who practice equity and justice
Allah only forbids you, those (for friendship) who fight against you regarding (your) faith (of Islam), and drive you out of your homes, and (those who) support (others) in driving you out, from turning to them (for friendship and protection). It is those who turn towards them (for friendship) that do wrong
O you who believe! When believing women come to you as refugees (and emigrants) examine (and verify) them (for their faith): Allah knows best as to their faith: Then if you ascertain that they are believers, then do not send them back to the unbelievers. They are not lawful (wives) for the unbelievers, nor are the (unbelievers) lawful (husbands) for them. But pay the unbelievers what they have spent (on their dowry). And there will be no sin (or blame) on you, if you marry them on payment of their dowry to them. But do not hold the guardianship of unbelieving women: Ask for what you have spent for their dowry, and let the (unbelievers) ask for what they have spent (on their dowers of women who have come to you). Such is the Judgment (the Command) of Allah: He judges (with justice) between you. And Allah is All Knowing (Aleem), All Wise (Hakeem)
And if any of your wives have gone (fallen in) to go to the disbelievers, then you succeed over them (by gaining victory over the disbelievers), then pay (from the booty) to those whose wives have gone, the equivalent of what they had spent (on their dowry). And fear Allah, in Whom you believe
O Prophet! When believing women come to you with an oath of their loyalty to you, (with a promise, pledging), that they will not associate in worship any other thing whatever with Allah, and that they will not steal, and that they will not commit adultery and that they will not kill their children, that they will not utter slander, fabricating falsehood from their hands and feet, and that they will not disobey you in any goodly just matter— Then, you accept their pledge (oath) of loyalty, and pray to Allah for the forgiveness (of their sins): Verily, Allah is Often Forgiving (Ghafoor), Most Merciful (Raheem)
O you who believe! Turn not (for protection) to people on whom is the Anger of Allah. About the Hereafter they are already in pain and suffering, just as the unbelievers are in pain and suffering, about those (buried) in graves
Whatsoever that is in the heaven and on earth, Glory Allah, and He is Almighty (Al-Aziz), the All Wise (Al-Hakeem)
O you who believe! Why do you say that which you do not do
Surely, it is most unpleasant, in Allah’s sight that you say that which you do not do
Truly Allah loves those who fight in His Cause in the battle array (rows), as if they were solid walls
And (remember), when Musa (Moses) said to his people: "O my people! Why do you hurt and insult me? Certainly, you know that I am a messenger of Allah (sent) to you?" So when they turned away (from the right path), Allah let their heart go wrong. And Allah does not guide those who are rebellious and disobedient
And (remember) when, Isa (Jesus), the son of Maryam (Mary), said: "O Children of Israel! I am a messenger of Allah (sent) to you, reaffirming Torah (the Torah, that came) before me, and giving the good news of a Messenger (reference to the Prophet Muhammad) to come after me, whose name shall be Ahmad." But when he (the Prophet) came to them with clear proofs, they said, "This is clearly magic (aimed at deception)
And who does greater wrong than the one who invents lies against Allah, while he is being invited to Islam? And Allah does not guide the wrongdoers
Their intention is to darken Allah’s Light (by bellowing) with their mouths: But Allah will complete (brightening) His Light. Even though the unbelievers may dislike (it)
It is He Who has sent His Messenger with Guidance and the Religion of Truth, that he may proclaim it over all religions even though the idolaters may dislike (it)
O you who believe! Shall I guide you to a trade (situation) that will save you from a painful penalty
That you believe in Allah and His Messenger (the Prophet), and that you strive very hard (to your best) in the Cause of Allah, with your property and your persons: That will be best for you, if you only knew
(If you do that), He will forgive you (for) your sins, and admit you to Gardens beneath which rivers flow, and to beautiful palaces in Eden (the Paradise) of eternity: That is indeed the highest Achievement
And another (favor) which you will love, —Help from Allah and a near (and quick) victory. So give glad tidings (and good news) to the believers
O you who believe!– Be(come) you, the helpers (in the Cause) of Allah: As Isa (Jesus), the son of Maryam (Mary), said to the followers (disciples); "Who will be my helpers to (the work of) Allah?" Said the followers (disciples), "We are Allah’s helpers!" Then a portion of the Children of Israel believed, and a portion disbelieved: So, We gave power to those who believed, against their enemies, and they became the ones who won
Whatever is in the heavens and on earth, glorifies of Allah,— The Sovereign King (Al-Malik), the Holy and Pristine (Al-Qudus), the Almighty (Al-Aziz), the All Wise (Al-Hakeem)
It is He Who has sent amongst the unlettered ones a messenger from among themselves to rehearse to them His Verses, to purify them, and to instruct them in (Book, Quran) Scripture and Wisdom— Verily, they had been openly in error before
And (He has sent the Prophet to) others among them (the Muslims ready to accept the Faith), who have not already joined them (the Muslims); And He is the Almighty (Al-Aziz), the All Wise (Al-Hakeem)
That is the Grace of Allah that He grants on whom He wills; And Allah is the Lord of the highest grace
The similarity of those who were entrusted and charged with the (obligations of the Judaic Law) Torah, but did not carry it (the trust) out, is (like) that of a donkey which carries voluminous scriptures (without understanding it). Evil is the likeness of people who falsify the Signs of Allah: And Allah guides not the wrongdoers
Say: "O you (Jewish people) who profess Judaism! If you think that you are friends to Allah, to the exclusion of (other believing) men, then express your desire for death, if you are truthful
But they will not express their desire (for death), because of the (deeds) their hands have sent on before them! And Allah knows well the wrongdoers
Say: "Verily, the death from which you run away will really overtake you: Then will you be sent back to the All—Knower (Al-Aalam) of things that are unseen and seen: And He will tell you the things that you did
O you who believe! When the call is recited for prayer on Friday (the day of assembly), hurry sincerely to the Remembrance of Allah, and leave behind the business (and traffic): That is best for you if you only knew
Then when the (Friday) prayer is finished, then may you may disperse through the land, and seek of the Grace and Bounty of Allah: And celebrate the Praises of Allah much and often (and without restriction): That you may be successful
And when they see some bargain or some amusement, they leave to run to it, and leave you standing. Say: "The (blessing) from the Presence of Allah is better than any amusement or bargain! And Allah is the Best to Provide (for all needs) (Khair-ur-Razikheen)
When the hypocrites come to you, they say, "We bear witness that you are indeed the Messenger of Allah." Allah knows that you are indeed His Messenger, and Allah bears witness that the hypocrites are indeed liars
They have made their oaths a way (to hide what they really are and) like this they stop (men) from the Path of Allah: Truly, their deeds are evil
That is because they had believed, and then they disbelieved; So a seal was set on their hearts; Therefore, they do not understand
And when you look at them, their bodies (that they show) please you; And when they speak, you listen to their words. They are like blocks of wood propped up, (unable to stand by themselves). They think that every cry is against them. They are the enemies, so (keep yourselves) beware of them. May the curse of Allah be on them! How are they deluded (away from the right truth)
And when it is said to them, "Come, that the Messenger of Allah may pray for your forgiveness (from Allah) for you," they turn aside their heads, and you could see them turning away their faces in arrogance
It is equal (all the same) for them whether you (O Prophet!) pray for their forgiveness or pray not for their forgiveness; Allah will not forgive them. Truly Allah guides not those who rebel and transgress
They are the ones who say: "Spend nothing on those who are with Allah’s Messenger, until they may disperse (and quit Medinah)." And to Allah belong the treasures of the heavens and the earth; But the hypocrites do not understand
They say: "If we return to Medinah, surely, the more honorable (element) will expel from there the weaker." But honor belongs to Allah and to His Messenger, and to the believers; But the hypocrites do not know
O you who believe! Let not your properties nor your children distract you from remembering Allah. If any act like this, the loss is their own
And spend something (in charity) out of the sustenance that We have bestowed on you, before death should come to any of you and he should say, "My Lord! Why did You not give me relief for a little while? I should then have given (largely) in charity, and I should have been one of those who do good (deeds)
And Allah grants relief to none when the appointed time (for it) has come; And Allah knows well of (all) that you do
Whatever is in the heavens and whatever is on earth, glorifies of Allah: His is the (entire) Dominion, and to Him belongs all the Praise (and thanks) and He is Able (Khadir) to do all things
It is He, Who has created you; Some of you are unbelievers, and some of you are believers: And Allah is All Seeing (Baseer) of all that you do
He has created the heavens and the earth in proper proportions, and has given you shape, and made your shapes beautiful: And to Him is the final return
He knows what is in the heavens and (what is) on earth; And He knows what you hide and what you reveal: And Allah is All Knower (Aleem) of what (secret) lies in the breasts (and hearts of men)
Has the story not reached you, of the disbelievers before you? And so they tasted the evil result of their conduct; And they had a painful penalty
That was because messengers came to them with clear proofs, but they said: "Shall (mere) human beings direct us?" So they rejected (the Message) and turned away. But Allah is Free (Ghani) of all Needs, worthy of all Praise (Hameed)
The unbelievers think that they will not be raised up (for Judgment), say: "O Yes! By my Lord, you shall surely be raised up: Then shall you be told (the truth) of all that you did, and that is easy for Allah
Therefore, believe in Allah and His Messenger, and in the Light that We have sent down. And Allah is All Aware (Khabir) of all that you do
The Day when He assembles you (all) for a Day of Assembly— That will be a day of mutual loss and gain (among you), and (for) those who believe in Allah and do righteous deeds— He will remove from them their sorrows, and He will admit them to Gardens beneath rivers flow, to live in there forever: That will be the supreme achievement
But those who reject Faith and treat Our Signs as lies, they will be companions of the Fire to live in there forever: And evil is that goal
No type of misfortune can occur, except by the permission of Allah: And if anyone believes in Allah, (Allah) guides his heart (towards right): And Allah is All Knowing (Aleem) of all things
And obey Allah, and obey His Messenger: But if you turn away, the duty of Our Messenger is only to announce (the Message) clearly and openly
Allah! There is no god but He: And in Allah (Alone), therefore, let the believers put their trust
O you who believe! Truly, among your wives and your children are (some that are) enemies to yourselves: So be aware of them! But if you forgive them and overlook, and cover up (their faults), Surely Allah is Often Forgiving (Ghafoor), Most Merciful (Raheem)
Your wealth and your children may be a trial: But in the Presence of Allah is the Highest Reward
So fear Allah as much as you can; Listen and obey; And spend in charity for the benefit of your own souls! And those saved from the selfishness for themselves— Then they are the ones who achieve abundance (and wealth)
If you loan to Allah a beautiful loan, He will double it to your (credit), and He will grant you Forgiveness: And Allah is Most ready to appreciate and reward (Shukoor), Most Forbearing (Haleem)
(Allah is the) All Knower (Aleem) of what is hidden and of what is open, the Almighty (Al-Aziz), the All Wise (Al-Hakeem)
O Prophet! When you (Muslims) divorce women, divorce them at their prescribed periods, and count their prescribed periods (accurately). (Note: the Prophet himself never divorced any of his wives.) And fear Allah, your Lord: And turn them not out of their houses, nor shall they (themselves) leave except in case they are guilty of some clear and serious (sexual) misconduct. And these are the set-limits by Allah. And whosoever transgresses the set-limits of Allah, does indeed wrong his (own) soul: You do not know if by chance, Allah will bring about some new situation (later on)
When they fulfill their appointed term, either take them back in a good (and honorable) manner or part with them in a good (and honorable) manner. And take for witness two persons from among you, blessed with (a sense of) justice, and establish the evidence (as if you are) before Allah. Such is the guidance given to him who believes in Allah and the Last Day. And for those who fear Allah, He (always) prepares a way out
And He provides for him by (means that) he could never imagine. And if anyone puts his trust in Allah, then (Allah) is sufficient for him. Surely, Allah will accomplish His Purpose. Truly, for all things Allah has appointed proper proportions
Such of your women who have passed the age of monthly courses, for them the prescribed period, if you have any doubts, (the period) is three months, and for those who have no courses (it is the same). And for those who carry (life within their wombs) their period is until they deliver their burden, and for he who fears Allah, He will make their path easy for him
That is the Command of Allah, which He has sent down to you: And if anyone fears Allah, He will remove his sorrows from him, and will increase his reward
Let the women live (during waiting) in the same style as you live, according to your means: Do not annoy them, so as to restrict them. And if they carry (life in their wombs), then spend (your sustenance) on them until they deliver their burden: And if they suckle your (offspring) for you, give them their recompense: And mutually consult together, according to what is just and reasonable. And if you find yourselves in difficulties for one another, let another woman suckle (the child) on the (fathers) behalf
Let the man of means spend according to his means: And the man whose resources are restricted, let him spend according to what Allah has given him. Allah puts no burden on any person beyond what He has given him. After a difficulty, Allah will soon grant relief
And how many towns (populations) that proudly opposed the command of their Lord and of His messengers; And have We called (them) to account— To severe account? And We imposed on them a strict punishment
Then they tasted the evil result of their conduct, and the end of their action was (their) total loss
Allah has prepared a severe punishment for them (in the Hereafter). Therefore fear Allah, O men of understanding— Those who have believed! Allah has indeed sent down to you a Reminder (and a Message; The Quran)—
A Messenger, who rehearses to you the Signs of Allah containing clear explanations, that he (the Prophet) may lead forth those who believe and do righteous deeds from the depths of darkness into light. And whosoever believe in Allah and do righteous good deeds, He (Allah) will admit him to Gardens beneath which rivers flow, to live in there forever; Allah has indeed granted for them a most excellent provision
Allah is He Who has created seven Orbits (of heavenly planets) and of the earth a similar number. His Command descends between and through them: That you may know that Allah has power over all things, and that Allah comprehends all things in (His) Knowledge
O Prophet! Why do you forbid what Allah has made lawful to you? You seek to please your wives. And Allah is Often Forgiving (Ghafoor), Most Merciful (Raheem)
Allah has already made possible for you, (O men), to absolve your oaths (in some cases): And Allah is your Protector, and He is All Knowing (Aleem), All Wise (Hakeem)
And (remember) when the Prophet told in privacy a matter to one of his wives (Hafsah), and she then says it (to another, ‘Aishah), and Allah made it known to him, he (the Prophet,) informed a part of it and questioned a part. Then when he (the Prophet) told her about it, she said, "Who told you this?" He said, "He (Allah, Aleem) told me; (He) Who knows and is Well-Acquainted (Khabir, with all things)
If you two turn in repentance to Him (Allah), with sincerity in your hearts; But if you support each other against him, truly Allah is his Protector, and Gabriel, and every righteous one among those who believe— And after that the angels —will support him
It may be, if he (the Prophet) divorced you (all) that Allah will give him in exchange wives better than you— Who submit (their wills), who believe, who are (devoutly) obedient, who turn to Allah in repentance, who sincerely worship (in humility) who travel (for their faith in Islam) and who fast— Previously married or virgins
O you who believe! Save yourselves and your families from a Fire whose fuel is men and stones, over which are (appointed) angels strong and severe, who do not hesitate (from executing) the commands they receive from Allah, but do (precisely) what they are commanded
(They will say) "O you unbelievers! Make no excuses this Day! You are only being punished for all that you did
O you who believe! Turn to Allah with sincere repentance: In the hope that your Lord will remove from you your sorrows and admit you to Gardens beneath which rivers flow— The Day that Allah will not disgrace the Prophet and those who believe with him, their light will run before them and on their right hands, while they say, "Our Lord! Perfect our light for us, and grant us forgiveness: Verily, You are Able (Khadir) to do all things
O Prophet! Strive (work) hard against the unbelievers and the hypocrites, and be firm against them. Their home is Hell— And (it is) an evil refuge (indeed)
Allah has set forth, for an example to the unbelievers, the wife of Nuh (Noah), and the wife of Lut (Lot); They were each under two of Our righteous servants, but they were untrue to their (husbands), and they gained nothing before Allah on their account, but they were told: "You enter the Fire along with (others) who enter
And Allah has set forth, as an example to those who believe the wife of Firon (Pharaoh): When she said: "My Lord! Build for me, in nearness to You, a mansion in the Garden, and save me from Firon (Pharaoh) and his (evil) actions, and save me from those who do wrong
And Maryam (Mary), the daughter of Imran, she guarded her chastity; And We breathed into (her body) of Our Spirit and she testified to the truth of the words of her Lord and the Books (of Revelation) and was one of the devout (servants)
Blessed be He in Whose hands is the Dominion; And He is All Powerful (Al-Khad'ir) Able to do all things
He Who created Death and Life, that He may test which of you is best in deed: And He is the Almighty (Al-Aziz), the Often Forgiving (Al-Ghafoor)
He Who created the seven heavens one above the other: You will see no want of proportion in the Creation of (Allah) Most Gracious (Rahman). So look again, do you see any flaw
Then look again and once again: (And) your vision will come back to you dull and disjointed, in a worn out condition
And indeed, We have decorated the lowest heaven with lamps, and We have made them (like) missiles to drive away the Satans, and have prepared for them the penalty of the blazing Fire
And for those who disbelieve in their Lord (Ar-Rab'i, and Cherisher) is the Penalty of Hell: And evil is (their) destination
When they are cast therein, they will hear the (terrible) sighing of its breath even as it blazes forth
It almost flares up in fury: Every time a group is cast therein, its keepers will ask, "Did no warner come to you
And they will say: "Yes, indeed a warner did come to us but we rejected him and said (to him), Allah did not send down any (Message): You are making a serious error
And they will also say: "Had we only listened or used our understanding, we should not (now) be among the companions of the blazing Fire
Then they will confess their sins: (But forgiveness will be far), so away with the dwellers of the blazing Fire
Verily, those who fear their Lord Unseen, for them is forgiveness and a great reward
And whether you hide your word in secret or make it known, He is the All Knowing (Al-Aleem), of what is in the breasts (men’s hearts)
Would He not know— He Who has created? And He is the Most Generous (Al-Lateef to His servants and He is) the All Aware (Al-Khabir)
It is He Who has made the earth manageable (and amenable) for you, so you may travel through its open lands and enjoy the gifts which He furnishes: And to Him is the Resurrection
Do you feel secure that He Who is in Heaven will not cause you to be swallowed up by the earth when it rumbles (as if it is an earthquake)
Or do you feel secure that He Who is in Heaven will not send against you a violent tornado (with gravel and stones) so that you shall know how (terrible) was My warning (to them)
And indeed men before them rejected (My warning): Then how (terrible) was My rejection (of them)
Do they not watch the birds above them, spreading their wings and folding them in? None can uphold them except (Allah) Most Gracious (Rahman). Truly, it is He who is All Seeing (Baseer) all things
Who is there besides (Allah) Most Gracious (Rahman) who can help you, (even if it was) an army? But the unbelievers are in nothing but a delusion (and serious mistake)
Or who is there who can give you sustenance if He were to withhold His provision? But, they (the unbelievers) knowingly continue in willful disbelief and escape (from the Truth)
Is then (the man) who walks headlong, with his face bitter and marred, better guided— Or the one who walks evenly on the Straight Path
Say: "It is He, Who has created you (and made you grow), and made for you the faculties of hearing, (and) seeing, (feeling with your) heart (and its kindness): Little thanks it is you give
Say: "It is He, Who has created you on the earth, and to Him shall you be gathered together
They ask: "When will this promise be (fulfilled)? If you are telling the truth
Say: "As to the knowledge of the time, it is with Allah Alone: I am (sent) only to warn plainly in public
At length, when they see it (the time) close at hand, painful will be the faces of the unbelievers, and it will be said (to them): This is (the Promise fulfilled), which you were asking for
Say: "Do you see? If Allah were to destroy me, and those with me, or if He bestows His Mercy on us— Yet who can deliver the unbelievers from a grievous Penalty
Say: "He is (Allah), Most Gracious (Rahman): We have believed in Him, and on Him have we put our trust: So, soon will you know which (of us) who is in serious error
Say: "Do you see?— That if your streams (in the underground earth), on some morning become lost, then who can supply you with clear-flowing water
Nu’n, (the Pen): By the Pen and by the (Record) which (men) write—
You (O Prophet!) are not, by the grace of your Lord, mad, insane or possessed
No (in reality), and surely, for you is a reward unfailing
And verily, you (are placed) on an exalted standard of character
Soon will you see, and they will see
Which of you is affected with madness
Surely, it is your Lord Who knows best, which (among men) has strayed from His Path: And He Knows (Aalam) best those who receive (true) Guidance
So listen not to those who deny (the Truth)
Their desire is that you should be suffering: So they would be suffering
Do not pay attention to the type of lowly man— Ready with (false) words
A slanderer, going about with hurtful falsehoods
(By habit) stopping (all) good, exceeding all bounds (and) deep in sin
Violent (and cruel) and in addition a shrewd manipulator—
Because he possesses wealth and numerous sons
When Our Signs are rehearsed to him, he cries; "Tales of the men of old (ancient peoples)
Soon shall We brand (the beast) on the nose
Surely, We have tried them as We tried the People of the Garden, when they swore to pluck the fruits of the (garden) in the morning
But made no reservation, (by saying: "Insha-Allah", or "If Allah Wills it)
Then there came on the (garden) a visitation from your Lord, (which swept away) all around while they were asleep
So the (garden) became, by the morning, like a dark desolate spot (whose fruit had been gathered)
As the morning broke, they called out, one to another—
Saying: "You go to your garden early in the morning, if you were to gather the fruits
And so they departed, conversing in secret low tones, (saying)
Let not a single needy person break in upon you into the (garden) this day
And they opened the morning, strong in an (unjust) claim
But when they saw the (garden) they said: "We have surely lost our way
Nay! Indeed we are denied (of the fruits of our labor)
Said one (person) more just than the rest of them: "Did I not say to you; Why not Glorify [Allah by saying, if Allah so Wills, (or Insha Allah]
They said: "Glory to our Lord! Surely, we have been doing wrong
Then they turned, one against another, in blame
They said: "Woe be unto us! We have indeed exceeded our limits
It may be that our Lord will give us in exchange a better (garden) than this: Truly, we do turn to Him (in repentance)
Such is the punishment (in this life); But surely, greater is the Punishment in the Hereafter— If only they knew
Surely, for the righteous, are the Gardens of Delight, in the Presence of their Lord
Shall We then treat the people of faith like (We treat) the criminals (and the peoples of sin)
What is the matter with you? How can you judge
Or do you have a Book through which you learn—
That you shall have, through it whatever you choose
Or have you promises with Us on oath reaching to the Day of Judgment, (providing) that you shall have whatever you shall demand
You ask of them, which of them will stand guarantee for that
Or have they some (false) ‘partners’ (in godhead referring the Nasrani’s idle notion of trinity)? Then let them produce their ‘partners’, if they are truthful
The Day that when the Shin (Allah’s Divine Self) shall be laid bare, and they shall be summoned to prostrate themselves but they (the hypocrites) shall not be able to do so—
Their eyes will be cast down— Intense shame will cover them: Seeing that they had been summoned before to prostrate themselves (in love and prayer to Allah and His admiration) while they were whole, (human beings in this world and they had refused)
Then leave Me Alone with those who falsify this Message: By degrees shall We punish them from directions they perceive not
A (long) time will I give for them: (But) truly Powerful is My plan
Or is it that you do ask them for a reward, so that they are not burdened with a load of debt
Or that the unseen (Ghaib) is in their hands, so that they can write it down
So wait with patience for the Decision of your Lord, and be not like the companion of the Fish when he cried out (to his Lord) in grief (see)
Had not the Grace from His Lord reached him, he would indeed, have remained (within the fish and not) cast off on the naked shore, while he was to be blamed
Thus did his Lord choose him and grant him the company of the righteous
And verily, the unbelievers would almost deceive with their eyes when they hear the Reminder (the Quran); And they say: "Surely, he is possessed
But it is nothing other than a Message to all creatures (men jinns' and all creations of) the worlds
The Sure Reality! (The Word and Retribution of Allah)
What is the Sure Reality
And what will make you realize what the Sure Reality is
The Samood (Thamud) and the ‘Ad people (treated) the stunning calamity as false
But the Samood (Thamud)— They were destroyed by a terrible storm of thunder and lightning
And the ‘Ad— They were destroyed by a furious wind extremely fierce
Which (wind) He (Allah) made it rage against them for seven nights and eight days continuously so that you could see all the people lying on their faces in its (path), as if they had been roots of hollow palm-trees tumbled down
Then do you see any of them left (still) living
And Firon (Pharaoh), and those before him and the cities overthrown, committed the same habitual sin
And (each) disobeyed the messenger of their Lord: So He punished them with a severe penalty
Verily, when the water (of Nuh's Flood) overflowed beyond its limits, We carried you (mankind) in the floating Ark
That We might make it a Message for you, that (your) ears (may listen) and retain (its extraordinary lessons) in memory
Then, when the blast is sounded on the Trumpet once
And the earth and its mountains shall be dislodged from their places and are crushed to powder at one stroke—
On that Day shall the Event (and Reality) become true
And the sky will be split apart, for that Day will be flimsy and torn apart
And the angels will be on its (the sky) sides, and on that Day eight (angels) will bear the Throne of your Lord above them
That Day shall you be brought to Judgment: Not (even) one act of yours that you hide will be hidden
Then he who will be given his record in his right hand will say: "Here! Read my record
Surely, I did really know that my account would (One Day) reach me
So, he will be in a life of (ultimate) joy
In a Garden placed high
The fruits in bunches there, will be low and near at hand
(The greeting will be:) "You eat and drink, with full satisfaction; Because of the good that you sent before you, in the days that are gone
And he who will be given his record in his left hand, will say: "I wish my record was not been given to me
And that I had never known what my account (contained)
Would that (death) had made an end of me
My wealth has been of no profit to me
My power has departed from me
(The command will be:) "Seize him and bind (shackle) him
And throw him in the blazing Fire
Further, make him march in a chain, whose length is seventy cubits (99-128 ft)
He was one, who would not believe in Allah, the Most Great (Al-Azeem)
And would not encourage the feeding of those in need
So, no friend does he have here this Day
Nor does he have any food (here) except the corruption from the washing of wound
Which none do eat except those who have sinned
So, I swear by what you see
And what you see not
That this is truly the word of an honorable Messenger (of Allah, the Prophet Muhammad)
It is not the word of a poet: Little it is you believe
Nor is it the word of a soothsayer (or a fortune teller): Little warning (and advice) it is, that you receive
(This is) a Message sent down from the Lord of the Worlds (Rab-ul-'Ala'meen)
And if he (the Messenger) were to invent any saying in Our Name
We should certainly have seized him by his right hand
And then We certainly would have cut off the artery of his heart
Nor could any of you withhold him (from Our Anger)
But truly this is a Reminder (the Quran) for those who fear Allah
And We certainly, know that there are among you those who reject (it)
But truly, it (the Reminder, this Quran) is a cause of sorrow for the unbelievers
And verily, it (the Quran) is the Truth of total certainty
So glorify the Name of your Lord the Most Great (Rab-ul-Azeem)
A questioner asked about the penalty to befall (yet to happen)—
Upon the unbelievers— There is none that can avert (the penalty)—
(A penalty) from Allah, Lord of the Ways of Ascent
The angels and the Spirit [Ruh, Gabriel] rise up to Him in a Day whose measure is fifty thousand years
Therefore you stay patient— With a good Patience (of beautiful contentment)
They see the (Day) indeed as a far-off (event)
But We see it (quite) near
The Day that the sky will be like molten brass
And the mountains will be like wool
And no friend will ask about a friend
Though they will be put in sight of each other— The sinners (only) wish will be that he could save himself from the penalty of that Day by (even offering) his children
His wife and his brother
And his relatives who sheltered him
And all, all that is on earth— So that it could save him—
By no means! Verily, it would be the Fire of Hell
Tearing out (his existence) right out of his skull
Inviting (all) those who turn their backs and turn away their faces (from the right)
And collect (wealth) and hide it (from use for Allah)
Truly, man was created very impatient—
Anxious and angry when evil touches him
And miserly when good reaches him—
Not so (are) those devoted to prayer—
Those who remain steadfast to their prayer
And those in whose wealth, is a recognized right (of Allah)
For the (needy) who ask and him who is prevented (for some reason from asking)
And those who hold to the Truth of the Day of Judgment
And those who fear the displeasure of their Lord—
Verily, their Lord’s displeasure is the opposite of peace and serenity:—
And those who guard their chastity (and sexuality)
Except from their wives and the (captive) whom their right hand possess— For (them), they are not to be blameworthy
But those who go beyond this are transgressors—
And those who respect their trusts and covenants
And those who stand firm in their testimonies
And those who safeguard (the sacredness) of their worship—
Such will be the honored ones in the Gardens (of Joy)
So, what is the matter with the unbelievers that they rush madly before you—
From the right and from the left in crowds
Does every man from them wish to enter the Paradise (and the Garden of Joy)
Definitely no! Verily, We have created them out of the (base matter) they know
But now, I swear by the Lord of (every point in) the Easts' and the Wests' that We can certainly—
Substitute them by others better (men) than them; And We are not to be defeated (in Our Plan)
So, leave them to sink in idle talk and play about— Until they encounter that Day of theirs that they have been promised
The Day when they will come out of from their graves in sudden haste as if they were rushing to a goal-post (fixed for them)—
With their eyes lowered in sadness— Fear and shame covering them (all over)! That is the Day that they were promised
Verily, We sent Nuh (Noah) to his people (with the command, saying): "Warn your people before there comes to them a painful penalty
He said: "O my people! Verily, I am an open warner to you
That you should worship Allah, fear Him and obey me
So He will forgive you your sins and give you relief for a fixed (and written) time: Verily, when the time is finished by Allah it cannot be put forward (changed or altered): If you only knew
He said: "O my Lord! Verily, I have called to my people night and day
But my calling them only increases (their) flight (from the right)
And verily, every time I have called to them, that You may forgive them, they have (only) pushed their fingers into their ears, covered themselves up with their clothes, grown firmer (against faith), and given themselves up to false pride
Then verily, I have called them loudly
Then verily, I have spoken to them in public and secretly in private
Saying to them, ‘Ask forgiveness from your Lord; Verily, He is Often Forgiving (Ghafa'r)
‘He will send rain to you in plenty
‘Give you increase in wealth and children; And grant to you gardens and grant to you rivers (of flowing water)
‘What is the matter with you, that you do not place your hope for kindness and long-suffering in Allah—
‘Seeing that it is He Who has created you in many different stages
‘Do you not see how Allah has created the seven heavens, one above another
‘And made the moon a light in the middle, and made the sun as a (glorious) lamp
‘And Allah has produced you from the earth, growing (you gradually)
‘And in the end, He will return you into the (earth) and raise you up (again at the Resurrection)
‘And Allah has made the earth for you as a carpet (a wide expanse, spread out)
‘That you may go about in there on broad and spacious roads?’
Nuh (Noah) said: "My Lord! They have disobeyed me, and they follow one whose wealth and children give them no increase but only loss
And they have planned a huge (and evil) plot
And they have said (to each other); ‘do not give up your gods: And do not give up Wadd, nor Suwa, neither Yaguth, nor Ya’uq, nor Nasr’—" (These are the false gods of the people of Nuh)
And indeed, they have already misled many; And (Allah,) You grant no increase to the wrongdoers but in wandering (aimlessly in their goal)
Because of their sins they were drowned (in the Flood), and they were made to enter the Fire (of punishment) and they found— Other than Allah, none to help them
And Nuh (Noah) said: "My Lord! Do not leave of the unbelievers, (even) a single one on earth
For, if You do leave (any of) them, they will only mislead Your servants and they will breed only the wicked ungrateful ones
My Lord! Forgive me, and my parents, and all who enter my house in Faith, and (all) believing men and believing women. And to the wrongdoers, You grant them no increase except in their loss
Say: "It has been revealed to me that an assembly of jinns' listened (to the Quran). They said, ‘Verily, we have really heard a Wonderful Recitation (this Quran)
‘It gives guidance to the Right (Path,) and we have believed in it (what is read, i.e., the Quran): We shall not join (in worship) any (gods) with our Lord
‘And unequaled is the Majesty of our Lord: He has taken neither a wife nor a son
“ ‘And that the foolish ones among us, who used to say terrible and worst lies against Allah
“ ‘And verily, we do think that no man or spirit (among jinns') should say anything that is untrue against Allah
“ ‘(It is) true, there were persons among mankind who took shelter with persons (other personifications) among the jinns', but they (only) increased them in their mistakes
‘And they (used to) think as you thought, that Allah would not raise up anyone (to Judgment)
‘And we have wanted to reach the (secrets of) heavens; But we found it filled with strong (and unfailing) guards and flaming fires (and shooting stars)
‘And verily, we used indeed, to sit there in (the hidden) places, to listen in but anyone who listens now will find a flaming fire (and shooting stars) watching him in hiding (to drive him away)
‘And we do not understand whether suffering is intended for those on earth, or whether their Lord intends to guide them to the right conduct
‘There are some among us who are righteous, and some (that are) the opposite:— We are assemblies (of jinns') having different ways
‘But we think that we cannot resist Allah all through the earth, nor can we resist Him by flight
‘And indeed for us, since we have listened to the Guidance, (from the Quran), we have believed therein: And anyone who believes in his Lord (he or she) has no fear, neither of a decrease in reward for the good deeds, nor an increase in punishment for the sins
‘And among us are some who submit their wills (to Allah as Muslims), and some who wander away from justice. Now those who submit their wills (as Muslims)— They have sought the right Path
‘And those who wander away (from the right Path)— They (are only fuel for fire of Hell ’ "—)
(And Allah’s Message is): "If they (the pagan) had (only) believed in Allah and walked on the (right) Path, we should certainly have granted (in kindness) to them (the) bountiful rain
That We might try them by that (means), and if anyone turns away from remembering his Lord, he will cause (for himself) to undergo a severe penalty
And the places of worship are for Allah (Alone): So do not pray to anyone along with Allah
And when the one devoted (the Prophet) to Allah stands forward to pray to Him, they (the jinns') just make around him a dense crowd as if sticking to one over the other (to listen)
Say: "I do no more than call upon my Lord, and I do not join any (false gods) with Him
Say: "It is not in my power to cause you harm, nor to bring you to right conduct
Say: "No one can save me from Allah's punishment, (if I were to disobey Him) nor should I find protection except in Him
Unless I proclaim what I receive from Allah and His Messages; For whoever that disobeyed Allah and His Messenger— Then verily, for him (the one who disobeys) is Hell:— He shall live in there forever
At length, when they see (with their own eyes) that which they are promised— Then will they know who is the one weakest as (their) helper and least important in point of numbers
Say: "I do not know whether the (punishment) which you are promised is near or whether my Lord will appoint for it a long time (later)
He (Allah, Alone) is All Knowledgeable of the Unseen, (Aalam-ul-Ghaib), nor does He make anyone familiar with His unseen mysteries—
Except a messenger whom He has chosen, and then He makes a band of watchers (angels) march before him and behind him
That he (the messenger) may know that they have (truly) brought and delivered the Messages of their Lord. And He surrounds (all with mysteries) that are with them, and takes account of every single thing
O you (Prophet! Clothed and) folded up in garments
Stand up (in prayer) by night, except a little (less)—
Half of it (the night), or less than that by a little
Or a little more; And recite the Quran in slow, stately (and) rhythmic tones
Verily, soon We shall send down upon you a weighty message
Truly, the rising by night is most powerful for governing (the soul) and most suitable for (understanding) the Word (of Prayer and Praise)
Verily, for you by the day, there is long (and hard) work with ordinary duties
And keep remembering the Name of your Lord and devote yourself to Him entirely
(He is) Lord of the east and the west: There is no god but He: Therefore take Him to be the disposer (Wakil) of (your) affairs
And have patience with what they say, and leave them with noble (dignity)
And leave Me Alone to deal with those in possession of the good things of life, who (still) reject the Truth; And (patiently) give them respite for a little while
With Us are shackles (to bind them), and a Fire (to burn them)
And a food that chokes, and a penalty that is painful
On the Day when the earth and the mountains will be in violent bang and the mountains will be like a heap of sand poured out and flowing down
Verily, We have sent to you (O men!) a Messenger, (the Prophet) to be a witness about yourselves, like We had sent a messenger (Musa) to Firon (Pharaoh)
But Firon (Pharaoh) did not obey the messenger; So We seized him with a stiff punishment
Then how shall you, if you deny (Allah) save yourselves against the punishment of Allah on a Day that will change children into gray-headed (old men)—
When the sky will be torn apart— His Promise certainly will come true
Surely, this is a (stern) warning and a guidance! Therefore, whoever wishes, let him take a (straight) Path to his Lord
Verily, (O Prophet), your Lord knows that you stand up (to prayer) a little less than two-thirds of the night, or half the night, or a third of the night, and so do some of those with you. And Allah measures the night and day in proper parts. He knows that you are not able to keep praying the whole night. So He has turned to you (in His Mercy), therefore you read the Quran as much as it may be easy for you. He knows that there may be (some) among you that are sick; Others traveling through the land, seeking of Allah’s Bounty; Yet others fighting in Allah’s Cause. You recite, therefore, as much of the Quran as may be easy (for you); And establish regular prayer and give regular charity; And loan to Allah a beautiful loan. And whatever good you send forward for your souls, you shall find it in Allah’s Presence: Yes, better and greater, in reward. And you seek the Forgiveness of Allah: Verily, Allah is Often Forgiving (Ghafoor), Most Merciful (Raheem)
O you (Prophet) wrapped up (in garments, blanket)
Get up and announce your warning
And you praise your Lord
And keep your clothes cleansed
And stay away from all pollution
And do not expect, in giving (the warning), any gain (for yourself)
And for (the duties) to your Lord be patient and unchanging
Then, when the trumpet is sounded
Truly, that will be — That Day, — A Day of suffering—
Far from being easy for the disbelievers
Leave Me Alone, to deal with the (creature) whom I created (bare and) alone
And then to whom I (reference to Allah, have) granted resources in plenty
And children to be by his side! —
And made (life) smooth and comfortable for him
Yet is he greedy that I should add (more and more), —
Nay! Truly, he has been opposing Our Signs
Soon will I visit him with a mountain of miseries
Verily, he thought and he plotted—
So, let him be the cursed (one)! How he plotted
And again let him be the cursed (one)! How he plotted
Then he thought (a little)
Then he and frowned (in anger) and glowered (with rage)
Then he turned back and was haughty
Then he said: "This is nothing but magic taken from the old
This is nothing but the word of a (mere) human being
Soon will I throw him into the Fire of Hell
And what will explain to you what is the Fire of Hell
Neither will it permit to tolerate, nor does it leave alone
Darkening and changing (and burning away) the color of man
Over it are nineteen (angels as the keepers)
And We have set none but angels as guardians of the Fire: And We have fixed their number (at 19 and it is so written in other Books) confirming it only as a trial for unbelievers— So that the People of the Book (Scripture) may become certain, and the believers may become convinced of their Faith— And that no doubts may be left for the People(s) of the Book (Scripture), and the believers; And that those in whose hearts is a disease (of hypocrisy) and the unbelievers may say, "What does Allah mean by this (symbol of 19 angels)?" Thus does Allah leave to wander those whom He pleases, and guide those whom He pleases. And none can know the forces of your Lord, except He. And this is no other than a warning to mankind
No, surely, by the moon
And by the night, as it leaves
And by the morning, as it shines forward—
Verily, this is but one of the mighty (events unfortunate to the disbelievers)
A warning to mankind—
To any one of you who chooses to move forward, or to those that fall behind—
Every soul will be (held) to account for its deeds
Except the companions of the right hand
(They will be) in Gardens (of happiness): They will question each other
And (ask) of the sinners
What led you into the Fire of Hell
They will say: "We were not from those who prayed
Nor were we from those who fed the poor
And we used to speak idle-talk with those who spoke against Truth
And we used to reject the Day of Judgment
Until there came upon us (the Hour) that is certain
There will be no pleading or intercession from (any) pleaders (to) profit them
Then what is the matter with them that they turn away from plain warning—
As if they were frightened wild donkeys
Running away from a lion
No doubt, each one of them wants to be given scrolls (of Revelation from Allah) spread out
By no means! But they fear not the Hereafter
Nay! Verily, this surely is a (stern) warning
Let any who will keep it (the warning) in memory
And they will not keep it in memory (mind) except as Allah wills: He is the One Who deserving the righteousness (with prayer and supplication to Him) and He is the One Who grants forgiveness (of the sins)
I swear by the day of Resurrection (when the dead shall be awakened)
And I swear by the spirit that blames itself
Does man think that We cannot assemble his bones together
Yes! We are able to put together the very tips of his fingers perfectly
But man wishes to do wrong (even) in the time (now) for the time that is to come
He asks: "When is the Day (of Resurrection)on which the dead shall be awakened
(Say:) "Soon, when the sight is bewildered
And the moon is buried in darkness
And the sun and moon are joined together,"—
On that Day man will say: "Where is the place to flee
By no means! (There will be) no place of safety
Before your Lord, that Day will be the place of rest
On the Day will man be told (all) that he put in front of him and all that he put behind
No! Man will be (a true) evidence against himself
Even though he may give his excuses
Move not your tongue (O Prophet!) about the (Quran) to hurry on with it (in its reading)
It is for Us to put it together and to make it known and be recited
And when We have it (known to you), then you follow its recitation (and form)
Then, it is for Us to explain it (and to make it clear)
But no, (you men!) you love the present life of this world
And neglect (and put aside) the Hereafter
Some faces that Day, will glow (in brightness and beauty):—
Looking towards their Lord
And some faces that Day, will be sad and sorry
In the fear that some back-breaking unhappy action was about to be started upon them
Yes, when (the soul) reaches the collar-bone (as it leaves the body)
And when there will be a cry (saying:), "Who is a magician (to put him together)
And he will conclude that it was (the time) of leaving (this world)
And one leg will be joined with another leg
(All) the drive (movement) on that Day will be to your Lord
But he disregarded (the truth), and he did not pray
And even more, he lied (against the truth) and turned away
Then he went back to his family with false pride
Suffering and sorrow to you (woe unto you, O man!), and a great suffering to you
Again, suffering and sorrow to you (woe unto you, O man!), and a great suffering to you
Does man think that he will be neglected (and left alone), (without purpose for which he was created)
Was he not a drop of sperm emitted (without any form)
Then did he become a leech-like clot; Then (Allah) made and gave (him) the right size and shape
He made two sexes, male and female of him
Does He not have, the Power to give life to the dead
Has there not been a long period of time, when man was nothing— (Not even) mentioned
Surely We have created man from a drop of mixed sperm and ovary fluids, in order to try him, so, We gave him (the gifts) of hearing and of sight
Verily, We showed him the Way: Whether he be thankful or not (rests upon his own will)
Verily, We have prepared for the disbelievers: Chains, shackles, and a blazing Fire
As to the righteous: They shall drink of a cup blended with Kafur—
A fountain where the devoted servants of Allah drink, making it flow in plenty
They make (their) vows, and they fear a Day whose sorrow spreads far and wide
And they feed for the love of Allah the needy, the orphan, and the captive and the needy,—
(Saying), "We feed you for the sake of Allah Alone, no reward do we want from you, nor thanks
Verily, We only fear a Day of painful suffering (that may arrive) from the side of our Lord
So, Allah will save them from the sorrow of that Day, and will spread over them a Light of beauty and a (cheerful) joy
And because they were patient and steady, He will reward them with a Garden and (clothes of) silk
Reclining in the (Garden) on raised couches (thrones), they will see there neither the sun’s (extreme heat) nor the moon’s (extreme cold)
And the shades of the (Garden) will come low over them, and the bunches (of fruit), there will hang low in (their) easy reach
And among them will be passed round containers of silver and glasses of crystal—
Crystal-clear, made of silver: They will determine the amount in there (according to their wishes)
And they will be given to drink from a Cup (of drink) mixed with Zanjabil (ginger)—
A fountain there called Salsabil
And round about them will (serve) youths of perpetual (freshness): If you were to see them you would think them as pearls scattered about
And when you look, it is there that you will see a joy and a magnificent kingdom (an immense constellation of beauty)
Upon them will be green garments of fine silk and heavy ornaments and they will be decorated with bracelets of silver; And their Lord will give to them to drink a cleansing drink, pure and holy
(It will be said to them:) "Surely, this is a reward for you, and your struggle (in life) is accepted and recognized
Verily, it is We Who have sent down the Quran to you by stages
Therefore be patient with uniformity to the Command of your Lord, and do not listen to the sinner or the thankless among them
And praise (with joy) the Name of your Lord every morning (Faj’r) and afternoon (Zuh’r and ‘Asr)
And part of the night prostrate yourself to Him (Maghrib and Isha prayers) and glorify Him (in predawn prayer) the long night through
Verily, as to these (thankless), they love the present life of this world, and put away behind them a heavy Day (that will be) hard
It is We Who created them, and We have made their joints strong; And when We (so) wish, We can replace them bringing others like them in their place
Verily, this (Verse of the Quran) is a warning: So whoever wishes, let him take a (straight) Path to his Lord
But you will not except as Allah wishes; Verily, Allah is Ever All Knowing (Aleem), All Wise (Hakeem)
He will admit to His Mercy whomever He wishes; But the wrongdoers— For them, He has prepared a painful penalty
By the (winds) sent one after another
Which then blow very hard in violent storms
And drive (things and the clouds) far and wide
Then separate them, one from another
Then spread a Message
Whether of justification or of warning
Surely, what has been promised to you (shall) really happen
Then when the stars lose their light (and glow)
And when the heaven is torn apart
And when the mountains are blown (to the winds) as dust
And when (all) the messengers are appointed a time (to gather)—
For what Day are these Signs (of Allah) deferred
For the Day of Sorting out (those destined to paradise from those destined to Hell)
And what will explain to you what is the Day of Sorting out
And, woe (sorrow and suffering), that Day for those (people) who reject the Truth
Did We not destroy the people before (for their evil ways)
So shall We make later generations to follow them
We deal with men of sin in this way
And, woe (sorrow and suffering), that Day for those (people) who reject the Truth
Have We not created you from a fluid (held) in low esteem
Then We placed in a place of rest (the womb), securely placed
For a period (of growth) depending (upon the need of the infant)
(And) We decide (the need); For We are the Best to decide (things)
And, woe (sorrow and suffering), that Day for those (people) who reject the Truth
Have We not made the earth (as a place) to bring together
For the living and the dead
And made mountains in there standing firm, high (in stature) and provided for you water that is sweet (to drink)
And, woe (sorrow and suffering), that Day for those (people) who reject the Truth
(It will be said to the disbelievers:) "You go to that which you used to reject (the Fire) as false
You go away to a shadow (of smoke climbing) in three columns
(Which gives) no shade with coolness, and is of no use against the fierce Fire
Verily, it (Hell) throws sparks (of fire huge) as Forts
As if there were (a string of) yellow camels (marching swiftly)
And, woe (sorrow and suffering), that Day for those (people) who reject the Truth
That will be a Day when they shall not be able to speak (for parts of the Day)
And they will not be allowed to bring out any excuse (begging for mercy)
And, woe (sorrow and suffering), that Day for those (people) who reject the Truth
That will be a Day of Judgment! We shall gather you and those before you together
Now, if you have a trick (or plot), use it against Me
And, woe (sorrow and suffering), that Day for those (people) who reject the Truth
Verily, as to the righteous (people) they shall be in (cool) shades and springs (of water)
And (they shall have) the fruits— All that they wish
(It will be said to the righteous:) "Eat you and drink you to your hearts content: Because you (have) worked (towards righteousness)
Verily, We certainly reward the doers of good deeds (Mushinun), in this way
And, woe (sorrow and suffering), that Day for those (people) who reject the Truth
(O you rejecters of the Truth,) you eat and enjoy yourselves (but) a little while, verily, you are the criminals (Mujrimun, and sinners)
And, woe (sorrow and suffering), that Day for those (people) who reject the Truth
And when it is said to them, "Bow yourselves (in Islam)!" They do not do so
And, woe (sorrow and suffering), that Day for those (people who reject the Truth)
Then, in what Message, after that (warning) will they believe
Concerning what are they asking
Concerning the great news
About which they cannot agree
Surely, they shall soon know
Surely, (but) surely, they shall soon know
Have We not made the earth as a wide expanse (as a bed)
And the mountains as pegs
And (have We not) created you in pairs
And made your sleep for rest
And made the night as an umbrella of peace
And made the day for finding livelihood
And (have We not) built over you the seven strong arches of the heavens
And placed (in there) a Light of brilliance
And do We not send down from the clouds water, in plenty
That We may produce with it, corn and vegetables
And gardens of rich growth
Surely, the Day of Judgment is an event appointed—
The Day that the Trumpet shall be sounded and you shall come forward in crowds
And the heavens shall be opened as if there were doors
And the mountains shall vanish, as if they were a mirage
Truly, Hell is like a place of ambush—
For those who fought (against Faith); (Their) place of eternal stay
They will live in there for ages
Nothing cool shall they taste there, nor any drink
Save a boiling fluid and a fluid, dark, grim, bitterly cold—
A fitting return (for their actions and for them)
Because, they did not fear any accounting (of their deeds)
But they (grimly) treated Our Signs as false
And all things, We have preserved on record
So taste you (the reward), because We shall not grant you any increase except in (your) punishment
Surely, For the righteous there will be a fulfillment of (their hearts) desires
Gardens enclosed, and grapevines
Companions of equal age
And a Cup full (to the very top)
In there, they shall not hear useless talk, vanity (and they shall not hear) anything false—
Reward from your Lord a gift, (large and) sufficient
(From) the Lord of the heavens and the earth, and all between— (Allah) Most Gracious (Rahman): None shall have power to argue with Him
The Day that the Spirit (Gabriel) and the angels will stand forth in ranks, none shall speak, except anyone who is permitted by (Allah): Most Gracious (Rahman), and he (the speaker) will say (only) what is correct
Surely, that Day will be the Reality: Therefore, let anyone who wishes, let him take a (straight) path returning to his Lord
Surely, We have warned you of a penalty near— The Day when man will see (the very acts) which his hands have sent forward, and the unbelievers will say, "Misery upon me! I may as well be (mere) dust
By the (angels) who tear out (the soul of the wicked, from its depths) with great force
By those who gently draw out (the soul of the blessed)
And by those who move along (the path of mercy)
Then move swiftly as if they were in a race
Then arrange (themselves) to complete (the Commands of Allah)—
One Day, when everything that can be improper will be in violent shock
Followed by often repeated (shocks)
That Day, hearts will be trembling with fear
The eyes (of men) will be looking down
(Now) they say: "What! Shall we really be returned to (our) former state
What! When we shall have become rotten bones
They say: "In that case, it will be a return with loss
But surely, there will be a single (far reaching) cry
And then watch! They will be (completely) awake (to receive Judgment)
Has the story of Musa (Moses) reached you
Listen, your Lord called out to him in the sacred valley of Tuwa:—
You go to Firon (Pharaoh), because he has indeed exceeded all limits
And say to him: ‘Would you (wish) that you should be purified (from sin)
‘And that I guide you to your Lord, so you should fear Him?’”
Then (Musa, Moses) showed him the great Sign
But (Firon) rejected it and disobeyed (the guidance)
Also, he turned his back, working hard (against Allah)
Then he collected (his men) and made a (false) claim
Saying, "I am your lord, most high
But Allah punished him, (and made) him an example— In the Hereafter, and in this life
Surely, in this (instance) is a warning with guidance for those who fear (Allah)
What! Are you (men) more difficult to make than the heaven (that Allah) has created
High above has He raised its cover, and He has given it order and perfection
At night He grants its darkness and its brightness He brings out (with light)
And more, He has extended the earth (far and wide also in the shape of an egg)
He draws out its moisture from there and its grazing lands
And the mountains He has firmly fixed—
For use and benefit to you and your cattle
Therefore, when the great and fearful (event) comes
The Day when man shall remember all what he struggled for
And the Fire of Hell shall be placed in full sight for (everyone) to see—
Then for those that had exceeded all limits
And (those who) had liked the life of this world
The home will be the Fire of Hell
And for those who had felt the fear of standing before their (Almighty) Lord and had restrained (their) souls from lowly desires
Their home will be the Garden
They will ask you (O Prophet) about the Hour— "When will be its appointed time
How are you (even included) in the announcement of its time
Your Lord (Alone) knows the limit fixed for it
You are only a warner for those who fear it
The Day when they see it, (it will be) as if they had waited for it a single evening, or the following morning
He frowned and turned away
Because there came to him (the Prophet), the blind man (breaking into the discussion)
But what could tell you (O Prophet) but that he (the blind man) might by chance grow (in his understanding)
Or that he may receive guidance and the teachings that might profit him
About the one who considers himself independent
You attend to him
Even though there is no blame on you if he did not grow (in understanding)
But to him (the blind man) who came to you with effort and sincerity
And with fear (in his heart)
Were you (O Prophet!) unmindful in shifting your attention to another
By no means (should it be so), because it is indeed a Message of Instruction
Therefore let anyone who makes up the mind, remember (and accept) it
(It is) in Books held in (great) honor
Supreme (in dignity) kept pure and holy
(Written) by the hands of holy scribes (writers) —
Blessed and just
Warning to man! What has made him reject Allah
From what stuff has He (Allah) created him
From a sperm-drop has He (Allah) created him, and then (He) makes him in proper size and shape
Then He (Allah) makes the path smooth for him
Then He (Allah) causes him to die and puts him in his grave
Then, when it is His (Allah’s) Will, He will raise him up (again)
By no means has he (man) fulfilled what Allah has commanded him to do
Then let man look at his food, (how We provide it)
For that We pour forth water in plenty
And We split the earth into pieces
And produce from there corn
And grapes and plants to eat
And olives and dates
And enclosed gardens thick with tall trees
And fruits and herbage (and the grasses)—
For you to use and (for your) help and for your cattle
At last! When there comes the deafening noise—
That Day man will run away from his own brother
And from his mother and his father
And from his wife and his children
On that Day each of the men, will have enough worry (of his own) to make him not mindful of the others
Some faces that Day will be shining
Laughing, being happy
And other faces that Day will be soiled with dust
Blackness will cover them
Such will be the rejecters of Allah, the unrighteous
When the sun (with its spacious light) is folded up
When the stars fall, losing their glitter
When the mountains vanish (like a dream)
When the she camels, ten months with young are left untended
When the wild beasts are herded together (in human habitations)
When the oceans boil over with a swell
When the souls are sorted out, (Put together, righteous with righteous and unrighteous with unrighteous)
When the female (infant) buried alive, is questioned
For what crime she was killed
When the books of deeds are laid open
When the world on High (heavens) is made visible
When the fire of Hell is set to a fierce burn
And when the Garden (of the heavens) is brought near
(Then) shall each soul know what it has brought (forward for this Day)
So truly I call to witness the receding stars that hide away
Go straight, or hide
And the night as it comes to an end
And the (glorious) morning as it moves away the darkness
Surely this is the Word of a most honorable Messenger, [The Angel, Gabriel]
Given the power with rank before the Lord of the Throne
With authority there, (and) faithful to his trust
And (O people!), your companion (the Prophet) is not one who is possessed
And without doubt he (the Prophet) saw him (the messenger from Allah) in the clear horizon
And he does not withhold purposely any knowledge of the unseen
And it is not the word of an evil spirit that is outcast
Where, then are you going
Surely, this is the Message to (all jinns and men, all the) creations of the worlds
(With guidance) to each one among you who is willing to walk straight
But you shall not make up your mind except as Allah the Lord of the worlds (Rab-Al-'Ala'meen), wishes
When the sky is split apart
When the stars fall thrown around
When the oceans are made to burst apart; (into one big ocean covering the earth)
And when the graves are turned upside down
(Then) each soul shall know what it has sent forward and (what it has) kept back
O man! What has misled you (away) from your Lord, Most Generous (Rab-ul-Kareem)
He, Who created you, given you the proper size and shape, and gave you a just basis (for thinking)
In whatever form He wishes, He puts you together
No! But you (men) reject the (Final) Judgment
But surely, over you (are angels) to protect you
Kind and honorable writing down (your deeds and works)
They know (and understand) all that you do
As for the righteous, they will be in Joy
And the wicked, they will be in Fire
Which they will enter on the Day of Judgment
And they will not be able to keep away from there
And what will explain to you what the Day of Judgment is
Again, what will explain to you what the Day of Judgment is
(It will be) the Day when no soul shall have power (to do) anything for another: Because on that Day, the Command will be wholly with Allah
Misery to those who deal in fraud, (woe be unto those who cheat)—
Those who demand full measure, when they have to receive by measure from men
But when they have to give by measure or weight to men give less than due
Do they not think that they will be called to account
On a Mighty Day
A day when (all) mankind will stand before the Lord of the worlds (Rab-ul-'Ala'meen)
But! Surely the record of the wicked is (saved) in prison register (Sijjin)
And what will explain to you what the prison register (Sijjin) is
(There is) a register (fully) written
Misery, on that Day, to those who deny—
Those who do not accept the Day of Judgment
And none can deny it except the transgressor beyond limits, the sinner
When Our Signs are read (and repeated) to him, he says, "Tales of old
By no means! But on their hearts is the stain of (the evil,) whatever they do
Surely, from the Light (of) their Lord, on that Day will they be blocked
Further, they will enter the Fire of Hell
Further, it will be said to them: This is the (reality), which you rejected as false
But no! Surely the record of the righteous is (saved) in register (‘Illiyyun) of the Supreme
And What will explain to you what the register (‘Illiyyun) of the Supreme is
There is a register (fully) written
To which bear witness those nearest (to Allah)
Truly the righteous will be in happiness
On Thrones (of dignity) they will be able to see a view (of all things)
You will recognize in their faces the beaming brightness of joy
Their thirst will be quenched with pure wine sealed
The seal will be musk: And for this let them desire, those who have true desires
With it will be (given) a mixture of drink from the Paradise (Tasnim, the nectar from the pure heavenly fountain)
A spring, from (which) drink those nearest to Allah
Those in sin used to laugh at those who believed
And whenever they passed by them, used to wink at each other (in mockery)
