And when they returned to their own people, they would return mocking
And whenever they saw them (those who believed), they would say, "Look! These are the people truly astray
But they (the unbelievers) had not been sent as keepers over them (those who believed)
But on this Day the believers will laugh at the unbelievers
On Thrones (of dignity) they will be able to see a view (of all things)
Will not the unbelievers have been paid back for what they did
When the sky is split apart
And obeys the command of its Lord, and it must do so
And when the earth is flattened out
And spills over what is within it and becomes empty
And obeys the command of its Lord, and it must do so
O you man! You are surely always moving towards your Lord painfully moving but you shall meet Him
Then he who is given his record (of deeds) in his right hand
Soon his account will be taken by an easy settlement
And he will be together with his people, happy
But he who is given his record behind his back
Soon will he cry for his lost soul
And, he will enter a blazing Fire
Truly, (on this earth) did he go about among his people, happy
Truly, did he think that he would not have to return (to Us)
But, for sure! His Lord was (always) watchful of him
So, I swear by the deep (red) glow of sunset
The night and its gathering (of nightly creatures)
And the moon in her fullness
You shall surely travel from one stage to the next (life to Hereafter)
What then, is the matter with them that they do not believe
And when the Quran is read to them, they do not fall prostrate
But being the opposite the unbelievers reject (Islam and the Message)
But Allah has full knowledge of what they do and think
So announce to them a painful penalty
Except to those who believe and work righteous good deeds: For them is a reward that will never be the end
By the sky, (displaying) the Zodiacal Signs
By the promised Day (of Judgment)
By the one who sees and that which is seen—
Accursed are (unbelievers, who become) the makers of the pit (of Fire)
Fire, (amply) supplied with fuel
Look! They sat by the (fire)
And they saw (all) that they were doing against the believers
And they ill-treated them (the believers) for no reason other than that they believed in Allah, exalted in Power (Aziz), Worthy of all Praise (Hameed)
(It is) to Him that belongs the dominion of the heavens and the earth! And Allah is the One to Witness (Shaheed) all things
Those who are cruel or unkind to (or draw into evil) the believing men and women, and do not turn in repentance, will have the penalty of Hell: They will have the penalty of the burning Fire
For those who believe and do righteous deeds, will be Gardens, beneath which rivers flow; That is the great success, (the fulfillment of all desires)
The Grip (and Power) of your Lord is truly Strong
It is He Who creates from the very beginning, and He can restore (life)
And He is the Often Forgiving (Al-Ghafoor) and full of loving Kindness (Al-Wadood)
(The Supreme) Owner of the Throne of Glory
(He) does everything (without an exception) that He intends to do
Has the story reached you (O Prophet,) of the forces—
Of Firon (Pharaoh) and of Samood (Thamud)
No! Yet the unbelievers reject (the Truth)
And Allah does overtake them from behind
No! (But) this is a Glorious Quran
(Written) within a tablet preserved (to last forever)
By the sky (the heaven) and by the Visitor by the night
And what will explain to you what is the Visitor by the night —
The shinning Star of intense brightness—
There is no soul without a Protector over it
Now, let man only think from what he is created
He is created from a drop emitted—
Proceeding from between the backbone and the ribs
Surely (Allah) is able to bring him back (to life)
The Day that (all) things secret will be tested
(Man) will have no power and no helper
By the sky that returns (with rains again and again)
And by the earth which opens out (for the gushing springs or the budding plants)—
Watch! This is the Word that separates out (Good from evil)
It is not a thing for amusement
As for them (the disbelievers), they are only plotting a scheme
And I am planning a Scheme
Therefore (O Prophet!) give a little time for the disbelievers: Bear with them gently (for a while)
Praise (and Glorify) the Name of your Lord, the Most High (Rab-Al-A'la)
Who has created, and given form and proper size
Who has prescribed laws (to live by) and given you guidance (in His Books)
And Who grows the (green and rich) pasture
And then makes it dry and stalky (with grain)
By small amounts We shall teach you (O Prophet!) To declare (the Message), so that you shall not forget
Except as Allah wills for He knows what is openly known and what is hidden
And We will make it easy for you (to follow) the simple (Path)
Therefore give guidance in case the guidance will profit (the listener)
The guidance will be received by those who fear (Allah)
But it will be avoided by those most unfortunate ones
Who will enter the great Fire
In which they will neither die nor live
But those will prosper, who purify themselves
And praise the Name of their Guardian-Lord and (purify their hearts) in prayer
But no! You prefer the life of this world
But the Hereafter is better and (it) lasts longer
And this is in the pages (of Books) of the very early (Revelations)—
The pages (of Books) of Ibrahim (Abraham) and Musa (Moses)
Has the story of The Overwhelming (Event) reached you
On that Day, some faces will suffer humiliation
Working (hard in) weariness—
While they enter the blazing Fire—
While they are given, from a boiling hot spring (fluid), to drink
No food will there be for them but a bitter Dhari’ (a dry, bitter and thorny fruit)
Which will neither nourish nor satisfy hunger
On that Day (other) faces will be joyful
Pleased with their struggle (of this life)—
In a Garden raised high
Where they shall not hear (empty words)
In there will be a bubbling spring
In there will be Thrones (of dignity), raised high
Cups placed (ready)
And cushions set in rows
And rich carpets spread out
Do they (the unbelievers) not look at the Camels, how they are made
And at the sky, how it is raised high
And at the mountains, how they are fixed firm
And at the earth, how it is spread out
Therefore you (O Prophet) give Guidance: For you are the one to guide
You are not the one to manage (men’s) affairs
But if any (one) turns away and rejects Allah—
Allah will punish him with a severe punishment
For to Us will be their return
Then it will be for Us to call them to account
By the break of Day; (Allah swears by the Dawn of the Day)
And by the ten nights
And by the even and odd (contrasted)
And by the night when it passes away; —
Is there (not) in these a Sign for those who understand
Do you not see how your Mighty Lord dealt with the people of 'Ad —
(And with the people) of the (city of) Iram, with lofty pillars
Which have not been reproduced in (all) the land
And with the people of Samood (Thamud) who cut out (huge) rocks in the valley? —
And with Firon (Pharaoh), the lord of stakes
These (people) exceeded beyond limits in the lands
And here (they) piled mischief (upon mischief)
Therefore did your Mighty Lord send upon them very lowly punishments
Because your (Mighty) Lord is (like a Guardian) on a watch tower
Now, as for man, when his Mighty Lord tries him (by) giving him honor and gifts then he (proudly) says, "My Mighty Lord has honored me
But when He tries him, (by) restricting his livelihood for him, then he says (in despair), "My Mighty Lord has put me to shame
No, no! But you do not honor the orphans
Nor do you encourage one another to feed the poor! —
And you (wrongly) consume inheritance— With all (the) greed
And you love wealth with passion
No! When the earth is pounded to powder
And your Mighty Lord arrives and His angels, rank upon rank
And on that Day, (when) Hell is brought (face to face), — On that Day will man remember, but (alas!) how will that remembrance profit him
He (the man) will say: "Ah! Had I sent forward (good deeds) for my (future) Life
Because, that Day, his punishment will be such like no one (else) can inflict
And His bonds will be such as none (else) can bind
(To the righteous person will be said:) "O, (you) soul, with (complete) rest and satisfaction
Come back you to your Lord,— Well pleased (yourself), and well-pleasing to Him
Enter you, among My devotees
Yes, enter you My heaven
I (reference is to Allah) do swear by this City (of Makkah)
That you (O Prophet!) are a free-man of this City
And (with the ties of) parent and child
Surely, We have created man into hard work and struggle
Does he think, that no one has power over him
He may (wrongly) say: "I have wasted away a lot of wealth
Does he think that no one oversees him
Have We not made a pair of eyes for him
And a tongue and a pair of lips
And shown him the two highways? (The right and the wrong)
But he has made no haste for the path that is hard
And what will explain to you the path that is hard
(It is) freeing the slave
Or the giving of food in a day of want (and suffering)
To the orphan with claims of relationship
Or to the needy one (down) in the dust
Then will he be (one) of those who believe and practices patience, (constancy, and self-restraint), and practices acts of kindness and compassion
Such are the companions of the right hand
But those who reject Our Signs, they are the (unhappy) companions of the left hand
On them will be the Fire covering over (all around)
By the sun and its glory
And by the moon as follows it
And by the Day as it reveals (the sun’s) glory
And by the night as it conceals it
And by the sky and its (wonderful) structure
And by the earth and its (vast) territory
And by the soul and the proportion and order given to it
And its enlightenment and to its wrong and to its right—
Truly, he succeeds who purifies it
And he fails who corrupts it
The people of Samood (Thamud) rejected (their messenger) by their excessive wrong-doing
Look, the most wicked man among them was chosen (for the crime)
But the messenger of Allah said to them: "It is a she-camel of Allah! And (let her) have her drink
Then they rejected him (as a false prophet) and they injured her (by cutting her hamstrings, See 54.29). So their Lord, on account of their crime, removed their traces and made them equal (in destruction)
And for Him, there is no fear of its consequences
By the night when it becomes dark
By the day as it appears in glory
By (the mystery of) the creation of male and female—
Surely, you seek diverse (goals)
So, he who gives (in charity) and fears (Allah)
And (in all sincerity) accepts and follows the best—
We will indeed make smooth for him the path to happiness
But he who is a greedy miser and thinks himself to be self-sufficient
And gives the lie to the best—
We will indeed make smooth for him the path to misery
(All of) his wealth will not profit him when he falls headlong (into the pit of Fire)
Surely, We take upon Ourselves to guide
And surely to Us (belong both) the end and the beginning
Therefore do I warn you of a Fire flaming fiercely
None shall reach it except the most unfortunate ones
Who give the lie to truth and turn their backs
But those most devoted to Allah shall be removed far from it—
Those who spend their wealth for increase in self-purification
And have in their minds no favor from anyone for which a reward is expected in return
But only the desire to seek the Approval of their Lord Most High (Rab-Al-A'la)
And soon will they attain (complete) satisfaction
By the Glorious Morning Light
And by the night when it is still—
Your Guardian-Lord has not forsaken you (O Prophet), nor is He displeased
And surely the Hereafter will be better for you than the present
And soon your Guardian-Lord will give you that with which you shall be well pleased
Did He not find you an orphan and give you shelter (and care)
And He found you wandering, and He gave you guidance
And He found you in need, and made you independent
Therefore, do not treat the orphan with harshness
Do not shut off the beggar (without listening gently)
But the Bounty of your Lord— Rehearse and proclaim
Have We not expanded for you (O Prophet), your chest
And removed from you your burden
The (burden) that did strained your back
And elevated your fame (in the eyes of the people)
So, surely with every difficulty there is relief
Surely, with every difficulty there is relief
Therefore, when you are free (from your immediate duties), continue in your hard work
And to your Lord, turn (all) your attention
By the Fig and the Olive
And the Mount of Sinai
And the City (Makkah) of security —
We have truly created man in the best of forms
Then We bring him down (to be) the lowest of the low—
Except those who believe and do righteous deeds: For they shall have an unfailing reward
Then what can be against you (O Prophet!), after this regarding the Judgment (to come)
Is Allah not the Wisest of judges
Proclaim! (And read aloud!) in the Name of the Lord and Cherisher, Who created —
Created man, out of a (mere) clot of thickened blood
Proclaim! And your Lord is Most Bountiful —
He, Who taught (the use of) the pen—
Taught man that which he did not know
Alas! But man oversteps all bounds
And he considers himself as self-sufficient
Surely, to your Lord is the return (of all)
Do you see the one who forbids—
A true believer when he (turns) to pray
Do you see if he (Our servant) is on (the path towards) Guidance?—
Or enjoins the right deeds
Do you see if he stands against (the Truth) and turns away
Does he not know that Allah sees
Let him become aware! If he does not stop, We will drag him by the hair (upon his forehead)—
A lying, sinful hair
Then, let him call (for help) to his own group (of friends)
We will call the angels of punishment (to deal with him)
But no! Do not pay any attention to him: But prostrate and bring yourself closer (to Allah)
We have indeed revealed this (Message, Quran) in the Night of Power (Honor)
And what will explain to you (O Prophet) what the Night of Power is
The Night of Power is better than a thousand Months
In it come down the angels and the Spirit (Gabriel) by Allah’s permission, to perform every task
Peace! (Be in) this (Night) until the rise of dawn
Those who reject (truth), among the People of the Book and among the polytheists, who were not going to depart (from their ways) until there should come to them Clear Evidence—
A Messenger (the Prophet) from Allah (is) rehearsing Scriptures, kept pure and holy
In which the laws (or decrees) are explained right and straight
The People of the Book did not make religious split until after there came to them Clear Evidence
And they have been commanded no more than this: To worship Allah, offering Him sincere devotion, being true (in faith); To establish regular prayer; And to practice regular charity: And that is the religion right and straight
Those who reject (truth), among the (Jewish and Christian) People of the Book and among the polytheists, will be in the Fire of the Hell, to live in there (for ever)— They are the worst of creatures
Those who have faith and do righteous deeds— They are the best of creatures
Their reward is with Allah: Gardens of Eternity, beneath which rivers flow; They will live in there for ever; Allah well pleased with them, and they (well pleased) with Him: All this (is) for such as (those who) fear their Lord and Cherisher
When the earth is shaken to her (deepest) Convulsion
And the earth throws up her burdens (from within)
And man cries (out in great pain): "What is the matter with her
On that Day will she (the earth) declare her news
For that (Day), your (Mighty) Lord will have given her (the earth) His (Allah's) Order
On that Day will men proceed in groups sorted out, to be shown the deeds that they (had done)
Then anyone who has done an atoms weight of good, Shall see it
And anyone who has done an atom’s weight of evil, Shall see it
By the (majestic horses) that run with panting (breath)
And strike sparks of fire
And raid (the enemy camp) with force in the morning
And raise the dust in clouds (for) the while
And penetrate straight in the middle (of enemies) in formation—
Truly, man is ungrateful to his (Almighty) Lord
And to that (fact), he bears witness (by his deeds)
And violent is he in his love for wealth
Does he not know— That when whatever is in the graves is thrown about
And whatever (locked up) in (human) breasts is made (clearly) evident—
That their Lord had been well aware of them, (even to) that Day
The (Day) of Noise and Chaos (of the Calamity)
What is the (Day) of Noise and Chaos
And what will explain to you what is the (Day) of Noise and Chaos
(It is) a Day when men will be like moths thrown about
And the mountains will be like torn wool
Then, he whose balance (of good deeds) will be (found) heavy—
Will be in a life of good pleasure and satisfaction
But he whose balance (of good deeds) will be (found) light—
Will have his home in a pit (of Fire)
And what will explain to you what this is
(It is) a Fire flaming fiercely
The rivalry among yourselves for piling up diverts you (from your duties)
Until you visit the graves
But no, you soon shall know (the reality)
Again, you soon shall know
No, if you were to certainly know within the mind (You would be aware)
You shall certainly see the Fire of Hell
Again you shall see it with the certainty of sight
Then, shall you be questioned that Day about the joy (that you indulged in)
By (the Promise of) time (infinite), ('Asr also refers to afternoon prayer, or later part in life)
Surely, man is in loss
Except such as (those who) have Faith and do righteous deeds and (join together) in the mutual teaching of truth, and of patience and perseverance
Grief (and warning) to every Scandal-monger and backbiter
Who piles up wealth and lays it by
Thinking that his wealth would make him last for ever
By no means! He will be sure to be thrown into that which breaks to pieces
And what will explain to you that which breaks to Pieces
(It is) the Fire of Allah lighted up (to a flame)
The (Fire) which rises to the heart
It shall be made to cover over them
In pillars stretched out
Did you not see how your Lord dealt with the companions of the elephant
Did He not make their evil plan go astray
And He sent against them flights of birds
Striking them (the companions of the elephant) with stones of baked clay
Then did He make them like an empty field of stalks and straw, (of which the corn) has been eaten up
For the agreements (promises) of security and safeguard (enjoyed) by Quraish
Their agreements (covering) journeys by winter and summer—
Let them adore the Lord of this House
(The One) Who provides them with food against hunger, and with security against fear (of danger)
Do you see the one who denies the Judgment (to come)
Then, it is such a (man) who repels (and discards) the orphan (with harshness)
And does not encourage the feeding of the needy
So, (this is a) warning to the worshippers
Who are neglectful of their prayers
Those who (only want) to be seen (by men)
But refuse (to offer even) the neighborly needs
To you (O Prophet!) We have granted the Fountain (of Abundance)
Therefore turn to your Lord in prayer and sacrifice
Because he who hates you— He will be cut off (from the hope of the future)
Say: "O you people who reject Faith
I do not worship what you worship
Nor will you worship what I worship
And I will not worship what you have been used to worship
Nor will you worship what I worship
To you be your religion, and to me (be) my religion
When the Help of Allah and victory (of Makkah) comes
And you (O Prophet!) see the people enter Allah’s Religion in crowds
Then celebrate the Praises of your Lord, and pray for forgiveness from Him: Surely, He is One Who accepts repentance, returning (in grace and kindness) with forgiveness
Perish the hands of the Father of Flame (Abu’-Lahab)! Perish he
(There is) no benefit to him (in the Hereafter) from all his wealth, and from all his gains
Soon he will be burnt in a Fire of burning Flame
And his wife shall carry the (crackling) wood, as fuel
A twisted rope of palm-leaf fiber around her (own) neck
Say: "He is Allah, The One (Ahad, and Only One)
Allah the Eternal (Samad, the Ever Enduring), the Absolute (and Alone)
He begets not (has no descendents, no children, none), nor was He (ever) begotten
And there is none like (or comparable) unto Him
Say: "I seek shelter (and security) with the Lord (Rab, the Cherisher) of the dawn
From the mischief of the created things
From the mischief of darkness as it spreads over
From the mischief of those who practice secret (and evil) arts as they blow into knots (riddles)
And from the mischief of the envious one as he practices envy
Say: "I seek shelter (and security) with the Lord (Rab, the Cherisher) of mankind
King (Malik, and Ruler) of mankind
God (Almighty) of mankind—
From the mischief of the Whisperer (of evil, the Satan, or the Evil one), who hides away (after his whisper)—
(The same Evil one) who whispers into the breasts (hearts) of mankind—
Among the jinns’ and among the men
